"DOTA_Item_Desc_Pennant_EG"	"購買這面隊旗來展現您對 Evil Geniuses 的支持！將它裝備在玩家裝備的「粉絲欄位」中就能向其他觀眾表明您支持的是哪一隊，還能夠升級旗幟來展現您的熱情！除此之外，裝備旗幟可以讓您在 Valve 所支援的比賽中觀賞您所支持的隊伍時能夠獲得掉落物品。EG 旗幟能夠與其他 EG 旗幟合成來升級您的隊伍旗幟等級，您的隊伍旗幟等級將會提升在觀賞職業聯賽中所支持隊伍的粉絲人數總值。"
"[english]DOTA_Item_Desc_Pennant_EG"	"Show your support for Evil Geniuses by buying this Team Pennant! Equip it in the 'fan slot' of your Player Loadout to show other spectators who you're rooting for. Upgrade it to show you mean business! In addition, equipping a pennant makes you eligible for item drops while you spectate your team's matches live during Valve supported tournaments.  EG pennants can be combined with other EG pennants to upgrade your Team Pennant fan level.  The level of your Team Pennant will increase the total fan value of the team when you are spectating a Tournament match."

在您的背包中雙擊或是點擊鑰匙右鍵然後選擇您要的藏寶箱來開啟。
在 2012 年 9 月 3 日之後此鑰匙將會變回普通鑰匙。"

After the end of September 3rd, 2012 this will become a normal key."
